goempty:
if (getequipid(EQI_ARMOR) == 2361||2362||2363||2632||2633||2750||2792||2793 && getequipcardid(EQI_ARMOR,2) > 0){
next;

}
else {
next;
if (getequipcardid(EQI_ARMOR,3) > 0 && countitem(20089) > 0){
set .@armor,getequipid(EQI_ARMOR);
set .@ref,getequiprefinerycnt(EQI_ARMOR);
set .@card1,getequipcardid(EQI_ARMOR,0);
set .@card2,getequipcardid(EQI_ARMOR,1);

delequip EQI_ARMOR;
getitem2 .@armor,1,1,.@ref,0,.@card1,.@card2,0,0;

mes "It was a great success!";
next;
mes "[ Brilliant Mechanic Ann ]";
mes "Enjoy your day!";
close;
end;
}
else if (.@gamble > 80 && .@gamble <= 100){

delequip EQI_ARMOR;
getitem2 .@armor,1,1,.@ref,0,.@card1,.@card2,0,0;

mes "Oh, no!";
next;
mes "[ Brilliant Mechanic Ann ]";
mes "The crysta didn't make it...";
mes "I'm so sorry.";
close;
end;
}
}
else {
mes "[ Brilliant Mechanic Ann ]";
mes "Are you kidding me?";
next;
mes "[ Brilliant Mechanic Ann ]";
mes "There's nothing here!";
close;
end;
}
}

set .@mirror,20043;
next;
mes "^FF0000WARNING^000000";
mes "All refine levels and cards compounded into your Tier II Weapon will be lost upon upgrading.";
menu "Flame Heart",firemirran,"Mystic Frozen",watermirran,"Great Nature",earthmirran,"Rough Wind",windmirran,"Crystal of Darkness",darkmirran,"1carat Diamond",neutmirran,"Hand of God",holymirran,"Little Ghost Doll",ghostmirran,"Poisonous Powder",poisonmirran,"Memento",undeadmirran;

firemirror:
if (countitem(40420) > 0 && getequipid(EQI_HAND_R) == .@mirror && countitem(20269) > 2 && countitem(994) > 99){
next;
delitem 40420,1;
delitem 6905,10;
delitem 994,100;
delequip EQI_HAND_R;
if (achievementexists(240034) == 0){
achievementcomplete(240034);
}
if (.@mirror == 20035) getitem 40300,1;
if (.@mirror == 20037) getitem 40330,1;
if (.@mirror == 20039) getitem 40320,1;
if (.@mirror == 20041) getitem 40350,1;
if (.@mirror == 20043) getitem 40380,1;
if (.@mirror == 20045) getitem 40310,1;
if (.@mirror == 20047) getitem 40340,1;
if (.@mirror == 20049) getitem 40370,1;
if (.@mirror == 20051) getitem 40360,1;
if (.@mirror == 20053) getitem 40410,1;
if (.@mirror == 20055) getitem 40390,1;
if (.@mirror == 20057) getitem 40400,1;
mes "Mirror Weapon acquired.";
close;
end;
}
else {
mes "[Attachment Interpreter]";
mes "Insufficient Materials.";
close;
end;
}

menu "Soul Decimator",geroldran,"Soul Brutalizer",justiceran,"Soul Shooter",kulotran,"Soul Orb",daniloran,"Argent Soul",paoloran,"Soul Breaker",jeraldran,"Soul Piercer",kurtran,"Soul Terminator",erikran,"Soul Cleaver",kamalran,"Soul Eater",astrearan,"Soulstrings",honestran,"Soulsoother",jonasran;

geroldran:
next;
mes "[Attachment Interpreter]";
mes "Warning! Weapon upgrade will remove all enhancements.";
menu "Continue",-;
if (countitem(6905) > 99 && getequipid(EQI_HAND_R) == 20059){
set .@item,20059;
set .@ref,getequiprefinerycnt(EQI_HAND_R);
set .@card1,getequipcardid(EQI_HAND_R,0);
set .@card2,getequipcardid(EQI_HAND_R,1);
set .@card3,getequipcardid(EQI_HAND_R,2);
set .@card4,getequipcardid(EQI_HAND_R,3);
next;
delitem 6905,100;
delequip EQI_HAND_R;
getitem2 39024,1,1,.@ref,0,.@card1,.@card2,.@card3,.@card4;
if (achievementexists(240037) == 0){
achievementcomplete(240037);
}
mes "[Attachment Interpreter]";
mes "Operation Success, New Soul Weapon Created.";
close;
end;
}
else {
next;
mes "[Attachment Interpreter]";
mes "Error, please try again.";
next;
mes "[Attachment Interpreter]";
mes "System Malfunction, closing intervals.";
close;
end;
}

mes "500 Dragon Scale";
mes "500 Lizard Frills";
mes "500 Draconian Wing";

if (countitem(39126) > 99 && countitem(39103) > 499 && countitem(39132) > 499 && countitem(39131) > 499 && getequipid(EQI_GARMENT) == 2554){
set .@garment,2554;
set .@ref,getequiprefinerycnt(EQI_GARMENT);

next;

achievementcomplete(240039);
}

end;
}
else {
next;
mes "[Attachment Interpreter]";

end;
}
